ṛṣiruvāca
revatī sumahābhāgā trailokyasyāpi sundarī 
tava bharyā varārohā tāṃ tvaṃ rājanna vetsi kim  MarkP 
rājovāca
subhadrāṃ śāntatanayāṃ kāverītanayāṃ vibho 
surāṣṭrajāṃ sujātāñca kadambāñca varūthajām  MarkP 
vipāṭhāṃ nandinīñcaiva vedmi bhāryāṃ gṛhe dvija 
tiṣṭhanti me na bhagavan revatīṃ vedmi kānviyam  MarkP 
ṛṣiruvāca
priyeti sāmprataṃ yeyaṃ tvayoktā varavarṇinī 
kiṃ vismṛtante bhūpāla 
ślāghyeyaṃ gṛhiṇī tava  MarkP 
rājovāca
satyamuktaṃ mayā kintu bhāvo duṣṭo na me mune 
nātra kopaṃ bhavān kartumarhatyasmāsu yācitaḥ  MarkP 
ṛṣiruvāca
tattvaṃ bravīṣi bhūpāla 
na bhāvastava dūṣitaḥ 
vyājahāra bhavānetadvahninā nṛpa coditaḥ  MarkP 
mayā pṛṣṭo hutavahaḥ ko 'syā bharteti pārthiva 
bhavitā tena cāpyukto bhavānevādya vai varaḥ  MarkP 
tadgṛhyatāṃ mayā dattā tubhyaṃ kanyā narādhipa 
priyetyāmantritā ceyaṃ vicāraṃ kuruṣe katham  MarkP 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato 'sāvabhavanmaunī tenoktaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ 
ṛṣistathodyataḥ kartuṃ tasyā vaivāhikaṃ vidhim  MarkP 
tamudyataṃ sā pitaraṃ vivāhāya mahāmune 
uvāca kanyā yatkiñcit praśrayāvanatānanā  MarkP 
yadi me prītimāṃstāta prisādaṃ kartumarhasi 
revatyṛkṣe vivāhaṃ me tatkarotu prasāditaḥ  MarkP 
ṛṣiruvāca
revatyṛkṣaṃ na vai bhadre candrayogi vyavasthitam 
anyāni santi ṛkṣāṇi subhru vaivāhikāni te  MarkP 
kanyovāca
tāta tena vinā kālo viphalaḥ pratibhāti me 
vivāho viphale kāle madvidhāyāḥ kathaṃ bhavet  MarkP 
ṛṣiruvāca
ṛtavāgiti vikhyātastapasvī revatīṃ prati 
cakāra kopaṃ kruddhena tenarkṣaṃ vinipātitam  MarkP 
mayā cāsmai pratijñātā bharyeti madirekṣaṇā 
na cecchasi vivāhaṃ tvaṃ saṅkaṭaṃ naḥ samāgatam  MarkP 
kanyovāca
ṛtavāk sa munistāta kimevaṃ taptavāṃstapaḥ 
na tvayā mama tātena brahmabandhoḥ sutāsmi kim  MarkP 
ṛṣiruvāca
brahmabandhoḥ sutā na tvaṃ bāle naiva tapasvinaḥ 
sutā tvaṃ mama yo devān kartumanyān samutsahe  MarkP 
kanyovāca
tapasvī yadi me tātastatkimṛkṣamidaṃ divi 
samāropya vivāho me tadṛkṣe kriyate na tu  MarkP 
ṛṣiruvāca
evaṃ bhavatu bhadrante bhadre prītimatī bhava 
āropayāmīndumārge revatyṛkṣaṃ kṛte tava  MarkP 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tatastapaḥ prabhāveṇa revatyṛkṣaṃ mahāmuniḥ 
yathāpūrvantathā cakre somayogi dvijottama  MarkP 
vivāhañcaiva duhiturvidhivad mantrayoginam 
niṣpādya prītimān bhūyo jāmātāramathābravīt  MarkP 
audvāhikante bhūpāla kathyatāṃ kiṃ dadāmyaham 
durlabhyamapi dāsyāmi mamāpratihatantapaḥ  MarkP 
rājovāca
manoḥ svayambhuvasyāhamutpannaḥ santatau mune 
manvantarādhipaṃ putraṃ tvatprasādād vṛṇomyaham  MarkP 
ṛṣiruvāca
bhaviṣyatyeṣa te kāmo manustvattanayo mahīm 
sakalāṃ bhokṣyate bhūpa dharmavicca bhaviṣyati  MarkP 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tāmādāya tato bhūpaḥ svameva nagaraṃ yayau 
tasmādajāyata suto revatyā raivato manuḥ  MarkP 
sametaḥ sakalairdharmairmānavairaparājitaḥ 
vijñātākhilaśāstrārtho vedavidyārthaśāstravit  MarkP 
tasya manvantare devān munidevendrapārthivān 
kathyamānān mayā brahman nibodha susamāhitaḥ  MarkP 
sumedhasastatra devāstathā bhūpatayo dvija 
vaikuṇṭhaścāmitābhaśca caturdaśa caturdaśa  MarkP 
teṣāṃ devagaṇānāntu caturṇāmapi ceścaraḥ 
nāmnā vibhurabhūdindraḥ śatayajñopalakṣakaḥ  MarkP 
hiraṇyalomā vedaśrīrūrdhvabāhustathāparaḥ 
vedabāhuḥ sudhāmā ca parjanyaśca mahāmuniḥ  MarkP 
vasiṣṭhaśca mahābhāgo vedavedāntapāragaḥ 
ete saptarṣayaścāsan raivatasyāntare manoḥ  MarkP 
balabandhurmahāvīryaḥ suyaṣṭavyastathāparaḥ 
satyakādyāstathaivāsan raivatasya manoḥ sutāḥ  MarkP 
raivatāntāstu manavaḥ kathitā ye mayā tava 
svāyambhuvāśrayā hyete svārociṣamṛte manum  MarkP 
ya eṣāṃ śṛṇuyānnityaṃ paṭhedākhyānamuttamam 
vimuktaḥ sarvapāpebhyo lokaṃ prāpnotyabhīpsitam  MarkP 
iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe raivatamanvantare pañcasaptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṣaṭsaptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
ityetat kathitaṃ tubhyaṃ pañca manvantaraṃ tava 
cākṣuṣasya manoḥ ṣaṣṭhaṃ śrūyatāmidamantaram  MarkP 
anyajanmani jāto 'sau cakṣuṣaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ 
cākṣuṣatvamatastasya janmanyasminnapi dvija  MarkP 
jātaṃ mātā nijotsaṅge sthitamullāpya taṃ punaḥ 
pariṣvajati hārdena punarullāpayatyatha  MarkP 
jātismaraḥ sa jāto vai māturutsaṅgamāsthitaḥ 
jahāsa taṃ tadā mātā saṃkruddhā vākyamabravīt  MarkP 
bhītāsmi kimidaṃ vatsa 
hāso yadvadane tava 
akālabodhaḥ sañjātaḥ kaccit paśyasi śobhanam  MarkP 
putra uvāca
māmattumicchati puro mārjārī kima na paśyasi 
antardhānagatā ceyaṃ dvitīyā jātahāriṇī  MarkP 
putraprītyā ca bhavatī sahārdā māmavekṣatī 
ullāpyollāpya bahuśaḥ pariṣvajati māṃ yataḥ  MarkP 
udbhūtapulakā snehasambhavāstrāvilekṣaṇā 
tato mamāgato hāsaḥ śṛṇu cāpyatra kāraṇam  MarkP 
svārthe prasaktā mārjārī prasaktaṃ māmavekṣate 
tathāntardhānagā caiva dvitīyā jātahāriṇī  MarkP 
svārthāya snigdhahṛdayā yathaivaite mamopari 
pravṛtte svārthamāsthāya tathaiva pratibhāsi me  MarkP 
kintu madupabhogāya mārjārī jātahāriṇī 
tvantu krameṇopabhogyaṃ mattaḥ phalamabhīpsasi  MarkP 
na māṃ jānāsi ko 'pyeṣa na caivāpakṛtaṃ mayā 
saṅgataṃ nātikālīnaṃ pañcasaptadinātmakam  MarkP 
tathāpi strihyase sāstrā pariṣvajasi cāpyati 
tāteti vatsa 
bhadreti nirvyalīkaṃ bravīṣi mām  MarkP 
mātovāca
na tvāhamupakārārthaṃ vatsa 
prītyā pariṣvaje 
na cedetadbhavatprītyai parityaktāsmyahaṃ tvayā  MarkP 
svārtho mayā parityakto yastvatto me bhaviṣyati 
ityuktvā sā tamutsṛjya niṣkrāntā sūtikāgṛhāt  MarkP 
jaḍāṅgabāhyakaraṇaṃ śuddhāntaḥ karaṇātmakam 
jahāra taṃ parityaktaṃ sā tadā jātahāriṇī  MarkP 
sā hṛtvā taṃ tadā bālaṃ vikrāntasya mahībhṛtaḥ 
prasūtapatnīśayane nyasya tasyādade sutam  MarkP 
tamapyanyagṛhe nītvā gṛhītvā tasya cātmajam 
tṛtīyaṃ bhakṣayāmāsa sā kramājjātahāriṇī  MarkP 
hṛtvā hṛtvā tṛtīyantu bhakṣayatyatinirghṛṇā 
karotyanudinaṃ sā nu parivartantathānyayoḥ  MarkP 
vikrānto 'pi tatastasya sutasyaiva mahīpatiḥ 
kārayāmāsa saṃskārān rājanyasya bhavanti ye  MarkP 
ānandeti ca nāmāsya pitā cakre vidhānataḥ 
mudā paramayā yukto vikrāntaḥ sa narādhipaḥ  MarkP 
kṛtopanayanaṃ tantu gururāha kumārakam 
jananyāḥ prāgupasthānaṃ kriyatāñcābhivādanam  MarkP 
sa gurostadvacaḥ śrutvā vihasyaivamathābravīt 
vandyā me katamā mātā jananī pālanī nu kim  MarkP 
gururuvāca
na tviyaṃ te mahābhāga 
janayitrī ruthātmajā 
vikrāntasyāgramahiṣī haiminī nāma nāmataḥ  MarkP 
ānanda uvāca
iyaṃ janitrī caitrasya viśālagramavāsinaḥ 
viprāgryabodhaputrasya yo 'syāṃ jāto 'nyato vacam  MarkP 
gururuvāca
kutastvaṃ kathayānanda 
caitraḥ ko vā tvayocyate 
saṅkaṭaṃ mahadābhāti kva jāto 'tra bravīṣi kim  MarkP 
ānanda uvāca
jāto 'hamavanīndrasya kṣatriyasya gṛhe dvija 
tatpatnyāṃ giribhadrāyāmādade jātahāriṇī  MarkP 
tayātra mukto haiminyā gṛhītvā ca sutañca sā 
bodhasya dvijamukhyasya gṛhe nītavatī punaḥ  MarkP 
bhakṣayāmāsa ca sutaṃ tasya bodhadvijanmanaḥ 
sa tatra dvijasaṃskāraiḥ saṃskṛto haiminīsutaḥ  MarkP 
vayamatra mahābhāga 
saṃskṛtā guruṇā tvayā 
mayā tava vacaḥ kāryamupaimi katamāṃ guro  MarkP 
gururuvāca
atīva gahanaṃ vatsa 
saṅkaṭaṃ mahadāgatam 
na vedmi kiñcinmohena bhramantīva hi buddhayaḥ  MarkP 
ānanda uvāca
mohasyāvasaraḥ ko 'tra jagatyevaṃ vyavasthite 
kaḥ kasya putro viprarṣe 
ko vā kasya nu bāndhavaḥ  MarkP 
ārabhya janmano nṝṇāṃ sambandhitvamupaiti yaḥ 
anye sambandhino vipra 
mṛtyunā sannivartitāḥ  MarkP 
atrāpi jātasya sataḥ sambandhoyo 'sya bāndhavaiḥ 
so 'pyastaṅgate dehe prayātyeṣo 'khilakramaḥ  MarkP 
ato bravīmi saṃsāre vasataḥ ko na bāndhavaḥ 
ko vāpi satataṃ bandhuḥ kiṃ vo vibhrāmyate matiḥ  MarkP 
pitṛdvayaṃ mayā prāptamasminneva hi janmani 
mātṛdvayañca kiñcitraṃ yadanyad dehasambhave  MarkP 
so 'haṃ tapaḥ kariṣyāmi tvayā yo hyasya bhūpateḥ 
viśālagrāmataḥ putraścaitra ānīyatāmiha  MarkP 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tataḥ sa vismito rājā sabhāryaḥ saha bandhubhiḥ 
tasmānnivartya mamatāmanumene vanāya tam  MarkP 
caitramānīya tanayaṃ rājyayogyaṃ cakāra saḥ 
saṃmānya brāhmaṇaṃ yena putrabuddhyā sa pālitaḥ  MarkP 
so 'pyānandastapastepe bāla eva mahāvane 
karmaṇāṃ kṣupaṇārthāya vimukteḥ paripanthinām  MarkP 
tapasyantaṃ tatastañca prāha devaḥ prajāpatiḥ 
kimarthaṃ tapyase vatsa 
tapastīvraṃ vadasva tat  MarkP 
ānanda uvāca
ātmanaḥ śuddhikāmo 'haṃ karomi bhagavaṃstapaḥ 
bandhāya mama karmāṇi yāni tatkṣapaṇonmukhaḥ  MarkP 
brahmovāca
kṣīṇādhikāro bhavati muktiyogyo na karmavān 
sattvādhikāravān muktimavāpsyati tato bhavān  MarkP 
bhavatā manunā bhāvyaṃ ṣaṣṭhena vraja tat kuru 
alante tapasā tasmin kṛte muktimavāpsyasi  MarkP 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
ityukto brahmaṇā so 'pi tathetyuktvā mahāmatiḥ 
tatkarmābhimukho yātastapaso virarāma ha  MarkP 
cākṣuṣetyāha taṃ brahmā tapaso vinivartayan 
pūrvanāmnā babhūvātha prakhyātaścākṣuṣo manuḥ  MarkP 
upayeme vidarbhāṃ sa sutāmugrasya bhūbhṛtaḥ 
tasyāñcotpādayāmāsa putrān prakhyātavikramān  MarkP 
tasya manvantareśasya ye 'ntare tridaśā dvija 
ye carṣayastathaivendro ye sutāścāsya tān śṛṇu  MarkP 
āpyā nāma surāstatra teṣāmeko 'ṣṭako gaṇaḥ 
prakhyātakarmaṇāṃ vipra 
yajñe havyabhujāmayam  MarkP 
prakhyātabalavīryāṇāṃ prabhāmaṇḍaladurdṛśām 
dvitīyaśca prasūtākhyo devānāmaṣṭako gaṇaḥ  MarkP 
tathaivāṣṭaka evānyo bhavyākhyo devatāgaṇaḥ 
caturthaśca gaṇastatra yūthagākhyastathāṣṭakaḥ  MarkP 
lekhasaṃjñāstathaivānye tatra manvantare dvija 
pañcame ca gaṇe devāstatsaṃjñā hyamṛtāśinaḥ  MarkP 
śataṃ kratūnāmāhṛtya yasteṣāmadhipo 'bhavat 
manojavastathaivendraḥ saṃkhyāto yajñabhāgabhuk  MarkP 
sumedhā virajāścaiva haviṣmānunnato madhuḥ 
atināmā sahiṣṇuśca saptāsanniti carṣayaḥ  MarkP 
ūrupuruśatadyumnapramukhāḥ sumahābalāḥ 
cākṣuṣasya manoḥ putrāḥ pṛthivīpatayo 'bhavan  MarkP 
etatte kathitaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ mayā manvantaraṃ dvija 
cākṣuṣasya tathā janma caritañca mahātmanaḥ  MarkP 
sāmprataṃ vartate yo 'yaṃ nāmnā vaivasvato manuḥ 
saptamīye 'ntare tasya devādyāstān śṛṇuṣva me  MarkP 
ya idaṃ kīrtayed dhīmān cākṣuṣasyāntaraṃ bhuvi 
śṛṇute ca labhet putrānārogyasukhasampadam  MarkP 
iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe ṣaṣṭhaṃ manvantaraṃ samāptam
adhyāyaḥ ṣaṭsaptatitamaḥ
saptasaptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
mārtaṇḍa rasyaverbhāryā tanayā viśvakarmaṇaḥ 
saṃjñā nāma mahābhāga tasyāṃ bhānurajījanat  MarkP 
manuṃ prakhyātayaśasamanekajñānapāragam 
vivasvataḥ suto yasmāttasmādvaivasvatastu saḥ  MarkP 
saṃjñā ca raviṇā dṛṣṭā nimīlayati locane 
yatastataḥ saroṣor'kaḥ saṃjñāṃ niṣṭhuramabravīt  MarkP 
mayi dṛṣṭe sadā yasmāt kuruṣe netrasaṃyamam 
tasmājjaniṣyase mūḍhe prajāsaṃyamanaṃ yamam  MarkP 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tataḥ sā capalāṃ dṛṣṭiṃ devī cakre bhayākulā 
vilolitadṛśaṃ dṛṣṭvā punarāha ca tāṃ raviḥ  MarkP 
yasmādvilolitā dṛṣṭirmayi dṛṣṭe tvayādhunā 
tasmādvilolāṃ tanayāṃ nadīṃ tvaṃ prasaviṣyasi  MarkP 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tatastasyāntu saṃjajñe bhartṛśāpena tena vai 
yamaśca yamunā ceyaṃ prakhyātā sumahānadī  MarkP 
sāpi saṃjñā ravestejaḥ sehe duḥ khena bhāminī 
asahantī ca sā tejaścintayāmāsa vai tadā  MarkP 
kiṅkaromi kva gacchāmi kva gatāyāśca nirvṛtiḥ 
bhavenmama kathaṃ bhartā kopamarkaśca naiṣyati  MarkP 
iti saṃcintya bahudhā prajāpatisutā tadā 
bahu mene mahābhāgā pitṛsaṃśrayameva sā  MarkP 
tataḥ pitṛgṛhe gantuṃ kṛtabuddhiryaśasvinī 
chāyāmayīmātmatanuṃ nirmame dayitāṃ raveḥ  MarkP 
tāñcovāca tvayā veśmanyatra bhānoryathā mayā 
tathā samyagapatyeṣu vartitavyaṃ yathā ravau  MarkP 
pṛṣṭayāpi na vācyante tathaitadgamanaṃ mama 
saivāsmi nāma saṃjñeti vācyametatsadā vacaḥ  MarkP 
chāyasaṃjñovāca
ākeśagrahaṇād devi 
āśāpācca vacastava 
kariṣye kathayiṣyāmi vṛttantu śāpakarṣaṇāt  MarkP 
ityuktā sā tadā devī jagāma bhavanaṃ pituḥ 
dadarśa tatra tvaṣṭāraṃ tapasā dhūtakalmaṣam  MarkP 
bahumānācca tenāpi pūjitā viśvakarmaṇā 
tasthau pitṛgṛhe sā tu kañcitkālamaninditā  MarkP 
tatastāṃ prāha cārvaṅgī pitā nāticiroṣitām 
stutvā ca tanayāṃ premabahumānapuraḥ saram  MarkP 
tvāntu me paśyato vatse dināni subahūnyapi 
muhūrtārdhasamāni syuḥ kintu dharmo vilupyate  MarkP 
bāndhaveṣu ciraṃ vāso nārīṇāṃ na yaśaskaraḥ 
manoratho bāndhavānāṃ nāryā bhartṛgṛhe sthitiḥ  MarkP 
sā tvaṃ trailokyanāthena bhartrā sūryeṇa saṅgatā 
pitṛgehe ciraṃ kālaṃ vastuṃ nārhasi putrike  MarkP 
sā tvaṃ bhartṛgṛhaṃ gaccha tuṣṭo 'haṃ pūjitāsi me 
punarāgamanaṃ kāryaṃ darśanāya śubhe mama  MarkP 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
ityuktā sā tadā pitrā tathetyuktvā ca sā mune 
saṃpūjayitvā pitaraṃ jagāmāthottarān kurūn  MarkP 
sūryatāpamanicchantī tejasastasya bibhyatī 
tapaścacāra tatrāpi vaḍavārūpadhāriṇī  MarkP 
saṃjñeyamiti manvāno dvitīyāyāmahaspatiḥ 
janayāmāsa tanayau kanyāñcaikāṃ manoramām  MarkP 
chāyāsaṃjñā tvapatyeṣu yathā sveṣvativatsalā 
tathā na saṃjñākanyāyāṃ putrayoścānvavartata  MarkP 
lālanādyupabhogeṣu viśeṣamanuvāsaram 
manustat kṣāntavānasya yamastasyā na cakṣame  MarkP 
tāḍanāya ca vai kopāt pādastena samudyataḥ 
tasyāḥ punaḥ kṣāntimatā na tu dehe nipātitaḥ  MarkP 
tataḥ śaśāpa taṃ kopācchāyāsaṃjñā yamaṃ dvija 
kiñcit prasphuramāṇauṣṭhī vicalatpāṇipallavā  MarkP 
pituḥ patnīmamaryādaṃ yanmāṃ tarjayase padā 
bhuvi tasmādayaṃ padāstavādyaiva patiṣyati  MarkP 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
ityākarṇya yamaḥ śāpaṃ mātrā dattaṃ bhayāturaḥ 
abhyetya pitaraṃ prāha praṇipātapuraḥ saram  MarkP 
yama uvāca
tātaitanmahadāścaryaṃ na dṛṣṭamiti kenacit 
mātā vātsalyamutsṛjya śāpaṃ putre prayacchati  MarkP 
yathā manurmamācaṣṭe neyaṃ matā tathā mama 
viguṇeṣvapi putreṣu na mātā viguṇā bhavet  MarkP 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
yamasyaitadvacaḥ śrutvā bhagavāṃstimirāpahaḥ 
chāyāsaṃjñāṃ samāhūya papraccha kva gateti sā  MarkP 
sā cāha tanayā tvaṣṭurahaṃ saṃjñā vibhāvaso 
patnī tava tvayāpatyānyetāni janitāni me  MarkP 
itthaṃ vivasvataḥ sā tu bahuśaḥ pṛcchato yadā 
nācacakṣe tataḥ kruddho bhāsvāṃstāṃ śaptumudyataḥ  MarkP 
tataḥ sā kathayāmāsa yathāvṛttaṃ vivasvataḥ 
viditārthaśca bhagavān jagāma tvaṣṭurālayam  MarkP 
tataḥ sa pūjayāmāsa tadā trailokyapūjitam 
bhāsvantaṃ parayā bhaktyā nijagehamupāgatam  MarkP 
saṃjñāṃ pṛṣṭastadā tasmai kathayāmāsa viśvakṛt 
āgataiveha me veśma bhavataḥ preṣiteti vai  MarkP 
divākaraḥ samādhistho vaḍavārūpadhāriṇīm 
tapaścarantīṃ dadṛśe uttareṣu kuruṣvatha  MarkP 
saumyamūrtiḥ śubhākāro mama bhartā bhavediti 
abhisandhiñca tapaso bubudhe 'syā divākaraḥ  MarkP 
śātanaṃ tejaso me 'dya kriyatāmiti bhāskaraḥ 
tañcāha viśvakarmāṇaṃ saṃjñāyāḥ pitaraṃ dvija  MarkP 
saṃvatsarabhramestasya viśvakarmā karavestataḥ 
tejasaḥ śātanañcakre stūyamānaśca daivataiḥ  MarkP 
iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe vaivasvatamanvantare saptasaptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
aṣṭasaptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tatastaṃ tuṣṭuvurdevāstathā devarṣayo ravim 
vāgbhiroḍyamaśeṣasya trailokyasya samāgatāḥ  MarkP 
devā ūcuḥ
namaste ṛksvarūpāya sāmarūpāya te namaḥ 
yajuḥ svarūparūpāya sāmnāndhāmavate namaḥ  MarkP 
jñānaikadhāmabhūtāya nirdhūtatamase namaḥ 
śuddhajyotiḥ svarūpāya viśuddhāyāmalātmane  MarkP 
variṣṭhāya vareṇyāya parasmai paramātmane 
namo 'khilajagadvyāpisvarūpāyātmamūrtaye  MarkP 
idaṃ stotravaraṃ ramyaṃ śrotavyaṃ śraddhayā naraiḥ 
śiṣyo bhūtvā samādhistho dattvā deyaṃ gurorapi  MarkP 
na śūnyabhūtaiḥ śrotavyametattu saphalaṃ bhavet 
sarvakāraṇabhūtāya niṣṭhāyai jñānacetasām  MarkP 
namaḥ sūryasvarūpāya prakāśātmasvarūpiṇe 
bhāskarāya namastubhyaṃ tathā dinakṛte namaḥ  MarkP 
śarvarīhetave caiva sandhyājyotsnākṛte namaḥ 
tvaṃ sarvametad bhagavan jagadudbhramatā tvayā  MarkP 
bhramatyāviddhamakhilaṃ brahmāṇḍaṃ sacarācaram 
tvadaṃśubhiridaṃ spṛṣṭaṃ sarvaṃ sañjāyate śuci  MarkP 
kriyate tvatkaraiḥ sparśājjalādīnāṃ pavitratā 
homadānādiko dharmo nopakārāya jāyate  MarkP 
tāvadyāvanna saṃyogi jagadetat tvadaṃśubhiḥ 
ṛcaste sakalā hyetā yajūṃṣyetāni cānyataḥ  MarkP 
sakalāni ca sāmāni nipatanti tvadaḍgataḥ 
ṛṅmayastvaṃ jagannātha 
tvameva ca yajurmayaḥ  MarkP 
yataḥ sāmamayaścaiva tato nātha 
trayīmayaḥ 
tvameva brahmaṇo rūpaṃ parañcāparameva ca  MarkP 
mūrtāmūrtastathā sūkṣmaḥ sthūlarūpastathā sthitaḥ 
nimeṣakāṣṭhādimayaḥ kālarūpaḥ kṣayātmakaḥ 
prasīda svecchayā rūpaṃ svatejaḥ śamanaṃ kuru  MarkP 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
evaṃ saṃstūyamānastu devairdevarṣibhistathā 
mumoca svaṃ tadā tejastejasāṃ rāśiravyayaḥ  MarkP 
yattasya ṛṅmayaṃ tejo bhavitā tena medinī 
yajurmayenāpi divaṃ svargaḥ sāmamayaṃ raveḥ  MarkP 
śātitāstejaso bhāgā ye tvaṣṭrā daśa pañca ca 
tvaṣṭraiva tena śarvasya kṛtaṃ śūlaṃ mahātmanā  MarkP 
cakraṃ viṣṇorvasūnāñca śaṅkavo 'tha sudāruṇāḥ 
pāvakasya tathā śaktiḥ śibikā dhanadasya ca  MarkP 
anyeṣāmasurārīṇāmastrāṇyugrāṇi yāni vai 
yakṣavidyādharāṇāñca tāni cakre sa viśvakṛt  MarkP 
tataśca ṣoḍaśaṃ bhāgaṃ bibharti bhagavān vibhuḥ 
tattejaḥ pañcadaśadhā śātitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā  MarkP 
tato 'śvarūpadhṛgbhānuruttarānagamat kurūn 
tadṛśe tatra saṃjñāñca vaḍavārūpadhāriṇīm  MarkP 
sā ca dṛṣṭvā tamāyāntaṃ parapuṃso viśaṅkayā 
jagāma saṃmukhaṃ tasya pṛṣṭharakṣaṇatatparā  MarkP 
tataśca nāsikāyogaṃ tayostatra sametayoḥ 
nāsatyadastrau tanayāvaśvīvaktravinirgatau  MarkP 
retaso 'nte ca revantaḥ khaḍgī carmo tanutradhṛk 
aśvārūḍhaḥ samudbhūto bāṇatūṇasamanvitaḥ  MarkP 
tataḥ svarūpamatulaṃ darśayāmāsa bhānumān 
tasyaiṣā ca samālokya svarūpaṃ mudamādade  MarkP 
svarūpadhāriṇīñcaimāmānināya nijāśrayam 
saṃjñāṃ bhāryāṃ prītimatīṃ bhāskaro vāritaskaraḥ  MarkP 
tataḥ pūrvasuto yo 'syāḥ so 'bhūdvaivasvato manuḥ 
dvitīyaśca yamaḥ śāpāddharmadṛṣṭirabhūt sutaḥ  MarkP 
kṛmayo māṃsamādāya pādato 'sya mahītale 
patiṣyantīti śāpāntaṃ tasya cakre pitā svayam  MarkP 
dharmadṛṣṭiryataścāsau samo mitre tathāhite 
tato niyogaṃ taṃ yāmye cakāra timirāpahaḥ  MarkP 
yamunā ca nadī jajñe kalindāntaravāhinī 
aśvinau devabhiṣajau kṛtau pitrā mahātmanā  MarkP 
guhyakādhipatitve ca revanto 'pi niyojitaḥ 
cchāyāsaṃjñāsutānāñca niyogaḥ śruyatāṃ mama  MarkP 
pūrvajasya manostulyaśchāyāsaṃjñāsuto 'grajaḥ 
tataḥ sāvarṇikīṃ saṃjñāmavāpa tanayo raveḥ  MarkP 
bhaviṣyati manuḥ so 'pi balirindro yadā tadā 
śanaiścaro grahāṇāñca madhye pitrā niyojitaḥ  MarkP 
tayostṛtīyā yā kanyā tapatī nāma sā kurum 
nṛpāt saṃvaraṇāt putramavāpa manujeśvaram  MarkP 
tasya vaivasvatasyāhaṃ manoḥ saptamamantaram 
kathayāmi sutān bhūpānṛṣīn devān surādhipam  MarkP 
iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe sāvarṇike manvantare vaivasvatotpattirnāmāṣṭasaptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ūnāśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
ādityā vasavo rudrāḥ sādhyā viśve marudgaṇāḥ 
bhṛgavo 'ṅgirasaścāṣṭau yatra devagaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ  MarkP 
ādityā vasavo rudrā vijñeyāḥ kaśyapātmajāḥ 
sādhyāśca maruto viśve dharmaputragaṇāstrayaḥ  MarkP 
bhṛgostu bhṛgavo devāḥ putrā hyaṅgirasaḥ sutāḥ 
eṣa sargaśca mārīco vijñeyaḥ sāmpratādhipaḥ  MarkP 
ūrjasvī nāma caivendro mahātmā yajñabhāgabhuk 
atītānāgatā ye ca vartante sāmpratañca ye  MarkP 
sarve te tridaśendrāstu vijñeyāstulyalakṣaṇāḥ 
sahasrākṣāḥ kuliśinaḥ sarva eva purandarāḥ  MarkP 
maghavanto vṛṣāḥ sarve śṛṅgiṇo gajagāminaḥ 
te śatakratavaḥ sarve bhūtābhibhavatejasaḥ  MarkP 
dharmādyaiḥ kāraṇaiḥ suddhairādhipatyaguṇānvitāḥ 
bhūtabhavyabhavannāthāḥ śṛṇu caitat trayaṃ dvija  MarkP 
bhūrloko 'yaṃ smṛtā bhūmirantarikṣaṃ divaḥ smṛtam 
divyākhyāśca tathā svargastrailokyamiti gadyate  MarkP 
atriścaiva vasiṣṭhaśca kāśyapaśca mahānṛṣiḥ 
gautamaśca bharadvājau viśvāmitro 'tha kauśikaḥ  MarkP 
tathaiva putro bhagavānṛcīkasya mahātmanaḥ 
jamadagnistu saptaite munayo 'tra nathāntare  MarkP 
ikṣvākurnābhagaścaiva dhṛṣṭaḥ śaryātireva ca 
nariṣyantaśca vikhyāto nābhāgāriṣṭa eva ca  MarkP 
karūṣaśca pṛṣadhraśca vasumān lokaviśrutaḥ 
manorvaivasvatasyaite nava putrāḥ prakīrtitāḥ  MarkP 
vaivasvatamidaṃ brahman 
kathitante mayāntaram 
asmin śrute naraḥ sadyaḥ paṭhite caiva sattama 
mucyate pātakaiḥ sarvaiḥ puṇyañca mahadaśnate  MarkP 
iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe sāvarṇike manvantare vaivasvatakīrtanaṃ nāmaikonāśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
aśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ 
krauṣṭukiruvāca
svāyambhuvādyāḥ kathitāḥ saptaite manavo mama 
tadantareṣu ye devā rājāno munayastathā  MarkP 
asmin kalpe sapta ye 'nye bhaviṣyanti mahāmune 
manavastān samācakṣva ye ca devādayaśca ye  MarkP 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
kathitastava sāvarṇiśchāyāsaṃjñāsutaśca yaḥ 
pūrvajasya manostulyaḥ sa manurbhavitāṣṭamaḥ  MarkP 
rāmo vyāso gālavaśca dīptimān kṛpa eva ca 
ṛṣyaśṛṅgastathā droṇastatra saptarṣayo 'bhavan  MarkP 
sutapāścāmitābhāśca mukhyāścaiva tridhā surāḥ 
viṃśakaḥ kathitāścaiṣāṃ trayāṇāṃ triguṇo gaṇaḥ  MarkP 
tapastaptaśca śakraśca dyutirjyotiḥ prabhākaraḥ 
prabhāso dayito dharmastejoraśmiścirakratuḥ  MarkP 
ityādikastu sutapā devānāṃ viṃśako gaṇaḥ 
prabhurvibhurvibhāsādyastathānyo viṃśako gaṇaḥ  MarkP 
surāṇāmamitābhānāṃ tṛtīyamapi me śṛṇu 
damo dānto ṛtaḥ somo vittādyāścaiva viṃśatiḥ  MarkP 
mukhyā hyete samākhyātā devā manvantarādhipāḥ 
mārīcasyaiva te putrāḥ kaśyapasya prajāpateḥ  MarkP 
bhaviṣyāśca bhaviṣyanti sāvarṇasyāntare manoḥ 
teṣāmindro bhaviṣyastu balirvairocanirmune  MarkP 
pātāla āste yo 'dyāpi daityaḥ samayabandhanaḥ 
virajāścārvavīraśca nirmohaḥ satyavāk kṛtiḥ 
viṣṇvādyāścaiva tanayāḥ sāvarṇasya manornṛpāḥ  MarkP 
iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe 'śītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ekāśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
sāvarṇiḥ sūryatanayo yo manuḥ kathyate 'ṣṭamaḥ 
niśāmaya tadutpattiṃ vistarād gadato mama  MarkP 
mahāmāyānubhāvena yathā manvantarādhipaḥ 
sa babhūva mahābhāgaḥ sāvarṇistanayo raveḥ  MarkP 
svārociṣe 'ntare pūrvaṃ caitravaṃśasamudbhavaḥ 
suratho nāma rājābhūt samaste kṣitimaṇḍale  MarkP 
tasya pālayataḥ samyak prajāḥ putrānivaurasān 
babhūvuḥ śatravo bhūpāḥ kolāvidhvaṃsinastathā  MarkP 
tasya tairabhavad yuddhamatiprabaladaṇḍinaḥ 
nyūnairapi sa tairyuddhe kolāvidhvaṃsibhirjitaḥ  MarkP 
tataḥ svapuramāyāto nijadeśādhipo 'bhavat 
ākrāntaḥ sa mahābhāgastaistadā prabalāribhiḥ  MarkP 
amātyairbalibhirduṣṭairdurbalasya durātmabhiḥ 
koṣo balañcāpahṛtaṃ tatrāpi svapure tataḥ  MarkP 
tato mṛgayāvyājena hṛtasvāmyaḥ sa bhupatiḥ 
ekākī hayamāruhya jagāma gahanaṃ vanam  MarkP 
sa tatrāśramamadrākṣīd dvijavaryasya medhasaḥ 
praśāntaśvāpadākīrṇaṃ muniśṣyopaśobhitam  MarkP 
tasthau kañcit sa kālañca muninā tena satkṛtaḥ 
itaścaitaśca vicaraṃstasmin munivarāśrame  MarkP 
so 'cintayat tadā tatra mamatvākṛṣṭacetanaḥ 
matpūrvaiḥ pālitaṃ pūrvaṃ mayā hīnaṃ puraṃ hi tat 
madbhṛtyaistairasadvṛttairdharmataḥ pālyate na vā  MarkP 
na jāne sa pradhāno me śūrahastī sadāmadaḥ 
mama vairivaśaṃ yātaḥ kān bhogānupalapsyate  MarkP 
ye mamānugatā nityaṃ prasādadhanabhojanaiḥ 
anuvṛttiṃ dhruvaṃ te 'dya kurvantyanyamahībhṛtām  MarkP 
asamyagvyayaśīlaistaiḥ kurvadbhiḥ satataṃ vyayam 
saṃcitaḥ so 'tiduḥ khena kṣayaṃ kośo gamiṣyati  MarkP 
etaccānyacca satataṃ cintayāmāsa pārthivaḥ 
tatra viprāśramābhyāse vaiśyamekaṃ dadarśa saḥ  MarkP 
sa pṛṣṭastena kastvaṃ bhoḥ hetuścāgamane 'tra kaḥ 
saśoka iva kasmāttvaṃ durmanā iva lakṣyase  MarkP 
ityākarṇya vacastasya bhūpateḥ praṇayoditam 
pratyuvāca sa taṃ vaiśyaḥ praśrayāvanato nṛpam  MarkP 
vaiśya uvāca
samādhirnāma vaiśyo 'hamutpanno dhanināṃ kule 
putradārairnirastaśca dhanalobhādasādhubhiḥ  MarkP 
vihīnaśca dhanairdāraiḥ putrairādāya me dhanam 
vanamabhyāgato duḥ khī nirastaścāptabandhubhaiḥ  MarkP 
so 'haṃ na vedmi putrāṇāṃ kuśalākuśalātmikām 
pravṛttiṃ svajanānāñca dārāṇāñcātra saṃsthitaḥ  MarkP 
kiṃ nu teṣāṃ gṛhe kṣemamakṣemaṃ kiṃ nu sāmpratam 
kathaṃ te kiṃ nu sadvṛttāḥ durvṛttāḥ kiṃ nu me sutāḥ  MarkP 
rājovāca
yairnirasto bhavāṃllubdhaiḥ putradārādibhirdhanaiḥ 
teṣu kiṃ bhavataḥ snehamanubadhnāti mānasam  MarkP 
vaiśca uvāca
evametadyathā prāha bhavānasmadgataṃ vacaḥ 
kiṃ karomi na badhnāti mama niṣṭhuratāṃ manaḥ  MarkP 
yaiḥ santyajya pitṛsnehaṃ dhanalubdhairnirākṛtaḥ 
patisvajanahārdaṃ ca hārdi teṣveva me manaḥ  MarkP 
kimetannābhijānāmi jānannapi mahāmate 
yatpremapravaṇaṃ cittaṃ viguṇeṣvapi bandhuṣu  MarkP 
teṣāṃ kṛte me niḥ śvāso daurmanasyaṃ ca jāyate 
karomi kiṃ yanna manasteṣvaprītiṣu niṣṭhuram  MarkP 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tatastau sahitau vipra taṃ muniṃ samupasthitau 
samādhirnāma vaiśyo 'sau sa ca pārthivasattamaḥ  MarkP 
kṛtvā tu tau yathānyāyaṃ yathārhaṃ tena saṃvidam 
upaviṣṭau kathāḥ kāściccakraturvaiśyapārthivau  MarkP 
rājauvāca
bhagavaṃstvāmahaṃ praṣṭumiccāmyekaṃ vadasva tat 
duḥ khāya yanme manasaḥ svacittāyattatāṃ vinā  MarkP 
mamatvaṃ gatarājyasya rājyāṅgeṣvakhileṣvapi 
jānato 'pi yathājñasya kimetanmunisattama  MarkP 
ayaṃ ca nikṛtaḥ putrairdārairbhṛtyaistathojjhitaḥ 
svajanena ca santyaktasteṣu hārde tathāpyati  MarkP 
evameṣa tathāhaṃ ca dvāvapyatyantaduḥ khitau 
dṛṣṭadoṣe 'pi viṣaye mamatvākṛṣṭamānasau  MarkP 
tatkimetanmahābhāga yanmoho jñāninorapi 
mamāsya ca bhavatyeṣā vivekāndhasya mūḍhatā  MarkP 
ṛṣiruvāca
jñānamasti samastasya jantorviṣayagocare 
viṣayaśca mahābhāga yāti caivaṃ pṛthak pṛthak  MarkP 
divāndhāḥ prāṇinaḥ kecidrātrāvandhāstathāpare 
kecid divā tathā rātrau prāṇinastulyadṛṣṭayaḥ  MarkP 
jñānino manujāḥ satyaṃ kintu te na hi kevalam 
yato hi jñāninaḥ sarve paśupakṣimṛgādayaḥ  MarkP 
jñānaṃ ca tanmanuṣyāṇāṃ yatteṣāṃ mṛgṛpakṣiṇām 
manuṣyāṇāṃ ca yatteṣāṃ tulyamanyattathobhayoḥ  MarkP 
jñāne 'pi sati paśyaitān pataṅgāñchāvacañcuṣu 
kaṇamokṣādṛtān mohātpīḍyamānānapi kṣudhā  MarkP 
mānuṣā manujavyāghra sābhilāṣāḥ sutān prati 
lobhātpratyupakārāya nanvetān kiṃ na paśyasi  MarkP 
tathāpi mamatāvarte mohagarte nipātitāḥ 
mahāmāyāprabhāveṇa saṃsārasthitikāriṇā  MarkP 
tannātra vismayaḥ kāryo yoganidrā jagatpateḥ 
mahāmāyā hareścaitattathā saṃmohyate jagat  MarkP 
jñānināmapi cetāṃsi devī bhagavatī hi sā 
balādākṛṣya mohāya mahāmāyā prayacchati  MarkP 
tayā visṛjyate viśvaṃ jagadetaccarācaram 
saiṣā prasannā varadā nṛṇāṃ bhavati muktaye  MarkP 
sā vidyā paramā mukterhetubhūtā sanātanī 
saṃsārabandhahetuśca saiva sarveśvareśvarī  MarkP 
rojovāca
bhagavan  kā hi sā devī mahāmāyeti yāṃ bhavān 
bravīti kathamutpannā sā karmāsyāśca kiṃ dvija  MarkP 
yatsvabhāvā ca sā devī yatsvarūpā yadudbhavā 
tat sarvaṃ śrotumicchāmi tvatto brahmavidāṃ vara  MarkP 
ṛṣiruvāca
nityaiva sā jaganmūrtistayā sarvamidaṃ tatam 
tathāpi tatsamutpattirbahudhā śruyatāṃ mama  MarkP 
devānāṃ kāryasiddhyarthamāvirbhavati sā yadā 
utpanneti tadā loke sā nityāpyabhidhīyate  MarkP 
yoganidrāṃ yadā viṣṇurjagatyekārṇavīkṛte 
āstīrya śeṣamabhajat kalpānte bhagavān prabhuḥ  MarkP 
tadā dvāvasurau ghorau vikhyātau madhukaiṭabhau 
viṣṇukarṇamalodbhūtau hantuṃ brahmāṇamudyatau  MarkP 
sa nābhikamale viṣṇoḥ sthito brahmā prajāpatiḥ 
dṛṣṭvā tāvasurau cograu prasuptaṃ ca janārdanam  MarkP 
tuṣṭāva yoganidrāṃ tāmekāgrahṛdayasthitaḥ 
vibodhanārthāya harerharinetrakṛtālayām  MarkP 
brahmovāca
viśveśvarīṃ jagaddhātrīṃ sthitisaṃhārakāriṇīm 
nidrāṃ bhagavatīṃ viṣṇoratulāṃ tejasaḥ prabhuḥ  MarkP 
tvaṃ svāhā tvaṃ svadhā tvaṃ hi vaṣaṭkāraḥ svarātmikā 
sudhā tvamakṣare nitye tridhā mātrātmikā sthitā  MarkP 
ardhamātrā sthitā nityā yānuccāryā viśeṣataḥ 
tvameva sandhyā sāvitrī tvaṃ devi jananī parā  MarkP 
tvayaiva dhāryate sarvaṃ tvayaitatsṛjyate jagat 
tvayaitatpālyate devi tvamatsyante ca sarvadā  MarkP 
visṛṣṭau sṛṣṭirūpā tvaṃ sthitirūpā ca pālane 
tathā saṃhṛtirūpānte jagato 'sya jaganmaye  MarkP 
mahāvidyā mahāmāyā mahāmedhā mahāsmṛtiḥ 
mahāmohā ca bhavatī mahādevī maheśvarī  MarkP 
prakṛtistvañca sarvasya guṇatrayavibhāvinī 
kālarātrirmahārātrirmoharātriśca dāruṇā  MarkP 
tvaṃ śrīstvamīśvarī tvaṃ hrīstvaṃ buddhirbodhalakṣaṇā 
lajjā puṣṭistathā tuṣṭistvaṃ śāntiḥ kṣāntireva ca  MarkP 
khaḍiganī śūlinī ghorā gadinī cakriṇī tathā 
śaṅkhinī cāpinī bāṇabhuśuṇḍī parighāyudhā  MarkP 
saumyā saumyatarāśeṣasaumyebhyastvatisundarī 
parāparāṇāṃ paramā tvameva parameśvarī  MarkP 
yacca kiñcit kvacidvastu sadasadvākhilātmike 
tasya sarvasya yā śiktiḥ sā tvaṃ kiṃ stūyate tadā  MarkP 
yayā tvayā jagatstraṣṭā jagatpātyatti yo jagat 
so 'pi nidrāvaśaṃ nītaḥ kastvāṃ stotumiheśvaraḥ  MarkP 
viṣṇuḥ śarīragrahaṇamahāmīśāna eva ca 
kāritāste yato 'tastvāṃ kaḥ stotuṃ śaktimān bhavet  MarkP 
sā tvamitthaṃ prabhāvaiḥ svairudārairdevi saṃstutā 
mohayaitau durādharṣāvasuro madhukaiṭabhau  MarkP 
prabodhañca jagatsvāmī nīyatāmacyuto laghu 
bodhaśca kriyatāmasya hantumetau mahāsurau  MarkP 
ṛṣiruvāca
evaṃ stutā tadā devī tāmasī tatra vedhasā 
viṣṇoḥ prabodhanārthāya nihantuṃ madhukaiṭabhau  MarkP 
netrāsyanāsikābāhuhṛdayebhyastathorasaḥ 
nirgamya darśane tasthau brahmaṇo 'vyaktajanmanaḥ  MarkP 
uttasthau ca jagannāthastayā mukto janārdanaḥ 
ekārṇave 'hiśayanāttataḥ sa dadṛśe ca tau  MarkP 
madhukaiṭabhau durātmānāvativīryaparākramau 
krodharaktekṣaṇāvattuṃ brahmāṇaṃ janitodyamau  MarkP 
samutthāya tatastābhyāṃ yuyudhe bhagavān hariḥ 
pañcavarṣasahasrāṇi bāhupraharaṇo vibhuḥ  MarkP 
tāvapyatibalonmattau mahāmāyāvimohitau 
uktavantau varo 'smatto vriyatāmiti keśavam  MarkP 
bhagavānuvāca
bhavanetāmadya me tuṣṭau mama vadhyāvubhāvapi 
kimanyena vareṇātra etāvaddhi vṛtaṃ mama  MarkP 
ṛṣiruvāca
vañcitābhyāmiti tadā sarvamāpomayaṃ jagat 
vilokya tābhyāṃ gadito bhagavān kamalekṣaṇaḥ  MarkP 
āvāṃ jahi na yatrorvo salilena pariplutā 
prītau svastava yuddhena ślāghyastvaṃ mṛtyurāvayoḥ  MarkP 
ṛṣiruvāca
tathetyuktvā bhagavatā śaṅkhacakragadābhṛtā 
kṛtvā cakreṇa vai cchinne jaghane śirasī tayoḥ  MarkP 
evameṣā samutpannā brahmaṇā saṃstutā svayam 
prabhāvamasyā devyāstu bhūyaḥ śṛṇu vadāmi te  MarkP 
iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe sāvarṇike manvantare devīmāhātmye madhukaiṭabhavadho nāma ekāśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
dvyaśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ 
ṛṣiruvāca
devāsuramabhūd yuddhaṃ pūrṇamabdaśataṃ purā 
mahiṣe 'surāṇāmadhipe devānāṃ ca purandare  MarkP 
tatrāsurairmahāvīryairdevasainyaṃ parājitam 
jitvā ca sakalān devānindro 'būnmahiṣāsuraḥ  MarkP 
tataḥ parājitā devāḥ padmayoniṃ prajāpatim 
puraskṛtya gatāstatra yatreśagaruḍadhvajau  MarkP 
yathāvṛttaṃ tayostadvanmahiṣāsuraceṣṭitam 
tridaśāḥ kathayāmāsurdevābhibhavavistaram  MarkP 
sūryendragnyanilendūnāṃ yamasya varuṇasya ca 
anyeṣāṃ cādhikārān sa svayamevādhitiṣṭhiti  MarkP 
svargānnirākṛtāḥ sarve tena devagaṇā bhuvi 
vicaranti yathā martyā mahiṣeṇa durātmanā  MarkP 
etadvaḥ kathitaṃ sarvamamarāriviceṣṭitam 
śaraṇaṃ vaḥ prapannāḥ smo vadhastasya vicintyatām  MarkP 
ṛṣiruvāca
itthaṃ niśamya devānāṃ vacāṃsi madhusūdanaḥ 
cakāra kopaṃ śambhuśca bhrukuṭīkuṭilānanau  MarkP 
tato 'tikopapūrṇasya cakriṇo vadanāttataḥ 
niścakrāma mahattejo brahmaṇaḥ śaṅkarasya ca  MarkP 
anyeṣāñcaiva devānāṃ śakrādīnāṃ śarīrataḥ 
nirgataṃ sumahattejastaccaikyaṃ samagacchata  MarkP 
atīva tejasaḥ kūṭaṃ jvalantamiva parvatam 
dadṛśuste surāstatra jvālāvyāptadigantaram  MarkP 
atulaṃ tatra tattejaḥ sarvadevaśarīrajam 
ekasthaṃ tadabhūnnārī vyāptalokatrayaṃ tviṣā  MarkP 
yadabhūcchāmbhavaṃ tejastenājāyata tanmukham 
yāmyena cābhavan keśā bahavo viṣṇutejasā  MarkP 
saumyena stanayoryugmaṃ madhyaṃ caindreṇa cābhavat 
vāruṇena ca jaṅghorū nitambastejasā bhuvaḥ  MarkP 
brahmaṇastejasā pādau tadaṅgulyor'katejasā 
vasūnāñca karāṅgulyaḥ kaubereṇa ca nāsikā  MarkP 
tasyāstu dantāḥ sambhūtāḥ prājāpatyena tejasā 
nayanatritayaṃ jajñe tathā pāvakatejasā  MarkP 
bhruvau ca sandhyayostejaḥ śravaṇāvanilasya ca 
anyeṣāṃ caiva devānāṃ sambhavastejasāṃ śivā  MarkP 
tataḥ samastadevānāṃ tejorāśisamudbhavām 
tāṃ vilokya mudaṃ prāpuramarā mahiṣārditāḥ  MarkP 
tato devā dadustasyai svāni svānyāyudhāni ca 
ūcurjayajayetyuccairjayantīṃ te jayaiṣiṇaḥ  MarkP 
śūlaṃ śūlādviniṣkṛṣya dadau tasyai pinākadhṛk 
cakraṃ ca dattavān kṛṣṇaḥ samutpādya svacakrataḥ  MarkP 
śaṅkhañca varuṇaḥ śaktiṃ dadau tasyai hutāśanaḥ 
māruto dattavāṃścāpaṃ bāṇapūrṇe tatheṣudhī  MarkP 
vajramindraḥ samutpādya kuliśādamarādhipaḥ 
dadau tasyai sahasrākṣo ghaṇṭāmairāvatād gajāt  MarkP 
kāladaṇḍādyamo daṇḍaṃ māśaṃ cāmbupatirdadau 
prajāpatiścākṣamālāṃ dadau brahmā kamaṇḍalum  MarkP 
samastaromakūpeṣu nijaraśmīn divākaraḥ 
kālakhca dattavān khaḍgaṃ tasyāścarma ca nirmalam  MarkP 
kṣīrodaścāmalaṃ hāramajare ca tathāmbare 
cūḍāmaṇiṃ tathā divyaṃ kuṇḍale kaṭakāni ca  MarkP 
ardhacandraṃ tathā śubhraṃ keyūrān sarvabāhuṣu 
nūpurau vimalau tadvad graiveyakamanuttamam 
aṅgulīyakaratnāni samastāsvaṅgulīṣu ca  MarkP 
viśvakarmā dadau tasyai paraśuñcātinirmalam 
astrāṇyanekarūpāṇi tathābhedyaṃ ca daṃśanam  MarkP 
amlānapaṅkajāṃ mālāṃ śirasyurasi cāparām 
adadajjaladhistasyai paṅkajaṃ cātiśobhanam  MarkP 
himavān vāhanaṃ siṃhaṃ ratnāni vividhāni ca 
dadāvaśūnyaṃ surayā pānapātraṃ dhanādhipaḥ  MarkP 
śeṣaśca sarvanāgeśo mahāmaṇivibhūṣitam 
nāgahāraṃ dadau tasyai dhatte yaḥ pṛthivīmimām  MarkP 
anyairapi surairdevī bhūṣaṇairāyudhaistathā 
saṃmānitā nanādoccaiḥ sāṭṭahāsaṃ muhurmuhuḥ  MarkP 
tasyā nādena ghoreṇa kṛtstramāpūritaṃ nabhaḥ 
amāyatātimahatā pratiśabdo mahānabhūt  MarkP 
cukṣubhuḥ sakalā lokāḥ samudrāśca cakampire 
cacāla vasudhā celuḥ sakalāśca mahīdharāḥ  MarkP 
jayeti devāśca mudā tāmūcuḥ siṃhavāhinīm 
tuṣṭuvurmunayaścaināṃ bhaktinamrātmamūrtayaḥ  MarkP 
dṛṣṭvā samastaṃ saṃkṣubdhaṃ trailokyamamarārayaḥ 
sannaddhākhilasainyāste samuttasthurudāyudhāḥ  MarkP 
āḥ kimetaditi krodhādābhāṣya mahiṣāsuraḥ 
abhyadhāvata taṃ śabdamaśeṣairasurairvṛtaḥ  MarkP 
sa dadarśa tato devīṃ vyāptalokatrayāṃ tviṣā 
pādākrāntyā natabhuvaṃ kirīṭollikhitāmbarām  MarkP 
kṣobhitāśeṣapātālāṃ dhanurjyāniḥ svanena tām 
diśo bhujasahasreṇa samantād vyāpya saṃsthitām  MarkP 
tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ tayā devyā suradviṣām 
śastrāstrairbahudhā muktairādīpitadigantaram  MarkP 
mahiṣāsurasenānīścikṣurākhyo mahāsuraḥ 
yuyudhe cāmaraścānyaiścaturaṅgabalānvitaḥ  MarkP 
rathānāmayutaiḥ ṣaḍbhirudagrākhyo mahāsuraḥ 
ayudhyatāyutānāñca sahasreṇa mahāhanuḥ  MarkP 
pañcāśadbhiśca niyutairasilomā mahāsuraḥ 
ayutānāṃ śataiḥ ṣaḍbhirvāṣkalo yuyudhe raṇe  MarkP 
gajavājisahasraughairanekairugradarśanaḥ 
vṛto rathānāṃ koṭyā ca yuddhe tasminnayudhyata  MarkP 
biḍālākṣo 'yutānāñca pañcāśadbhirathāyutaiḥ 
yuyudhe saṃyuge tatra rathānāṃ parivāritaḥ  MarkP 
vṛtaḥ kālo rathānāñca raṇe pañcāśatāyutaiḥ 
yuyudhe saṃyuge tatra tāvadbhiḥ parivāritaḥ  MarkP 
anye ca tatrāyutaśo rathanāgahayairvṛtāḥ 
yuyudhuḥ saṃyuge devyā saha tatra mahāsurāḥ  MarkP 
koṭikoṭisahasraistu rathānāṃ dantināṃ tathā 
hayānāñca vṛto yuddhe tatrābhūnmahiṣāsuraḥ  MarkP 
tomarairbhindipālaiśca śaktibhirmusalaistathā 
yuyudhuḥ saṃyuge devyā khaḍgaiḥ paraśupaṭṭiśaiḥ  MarkP 
kecicca cikṣipuḥ śaktīḥ kecit pāśāṃstathāpare 
devīṃ khaḍgaprahāraistu te tāṃ hantuṃ pracakramuḥ  MarkP 
sāpi devī tatastāni śastrāṇyastrāṇi caṇḍikā 
līlayaiva praciccheda nijaśastrāstravarṣiṇī  MarkP 
anāyastānanā devī stūyamānā surarṣibhiḥ 
mumocāsuradeheṣu śastrāṇyastrāṇi ceśvarī  MarkP 
so 'pi kruddho dhutasaṭo devyā vāhanakeśarī 
cacārāsurasainyeṣu vaneṣviva hutāśanaḥ  MarkP 
niśvasānmumuce yāṃśca yudhyamānā raṇe 'mbikā 
ta eva sadyaḥ sambhūtā gaṇāḥ śatasahasraśaḥ  MarkP 
yuyudhuste paraśubhirbhindipālāsipaṭṭiśaiḥ 
nāśayanto 'suragaṇān devīśaktyupabṛṃhitāḥ  MarkP 
avādayanta paṭahān gaṇāḥ śaṅkhāṃstathāpare 
mṛdaṅgāṃśca tathaivānye tasmin yuddhamahotsave  MarkP 
tato devī triśūlena gadayā śaktivṛṣṭibhiḥ 
śaḍgādibhiśca śataśo nijaghāna mahāsurān  MarkP 
pātayāmāsa caivānyān ghaṇṭāsvanavimohitān 
asurān bhuvi pāśena baddhvā cānyānakarṣayat  MarkP 
kecid dvidhā kṛtāstīkṣṇaiḥ khaḍgapātaistathāpare 
vipothitā nipātena gadayā bhuvi śerate  MarkP 
vemuśca kecidrudhiraṃ musale bhṛśaṃ hatāḥ 
kecinnapātitā bhūmau bhinnāḥ śūlena vakṣasi  MarkP 
nirantarāḥ śaraugheṇa kṛtāḥ kecidraṇājire 
śailānukāriṇaḥ prāṇān mumucustridaśārdanāḥ  MarkP 
keṣāñcidvāhavaśchinnāśchinnagrīvāstathāpare 
śirāṃsi peturanyeṣāmanye madhye vidāritāḥ  MarkP 
vicchinnajaṅghāstvapare petururvyāṃ mahāsurāḥ 
ekabāhvakṣicaraṇāḥ keciddevyā dvidhā kṛtāḥ  MarkP 
chinne 'pi cānye śirasi patitāḥ punarutthitāḥ 
kabandhā yuyudhurdevyā gṛhītaparamāyudhāḥ  MarkP 
nanṛtuścāpare tatra yuddhe tūryalayāśritāḥ 
kabandhāśchinnakhirasaḥ khaḍgaśaktyṛṣṭipāṇayaḥ  MarkP 
tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti bhāṣanto devīmanye mahāsurāḥ
rudhiraughaviluptāṅgāḥ saṃgrāme lomaharṣaṇe  MarkP 
pātitai rathanāgāśvairasuraiśca vasundharā 
agamyā sābhavat tatra yatrābhūt sa mahāraṇaḥ  MarkP 
śoṇitaughā mahānadyaḥ sadyastatra visustruvuḥ 
madhye cāsurasainyasya vāraṇāsuravājinām  MarkP 
kṣaṇena tanmahāsainyamasurāṇāṃ tathāmbikā 
ninye kṣayaṃ yathā vahnistṛṇadārumahācayam  MarkP 
sa ca siṃho mahānādamutsṛjan dhutakesaraḥ 
śarīrebhyo 'marārīṇāmasūniva vicinvati  MarkP 
devyā gaṇaiśca taistatra kṛtaṃ yuddhaṃ tathāsuraiḥ 
yathaiṣāṃ tutuṣurdevāḥ puṣpavṛṣṭimuco divi  MarkP 
iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyamahāpurāṇe sāvarṇike manvantare devīmāhātmye mahiṣāsurasainyavadho nāma dvyaśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
tryaśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ 
ṛṣiruvāca
nihanyamānaṃ tatsainyamavalākya mahāsuraḥ 
senānīścikṣuraḥ kopādyayau yoddhumathāmbikām  MarkP 
sa devīṃ śaravarṣeṇa vavarṣa samare 'suraḥ 
yathā merugireḥ śṛṅgaṃ toyavarṣeṇa toyadaḥ  MarkP 
tasya cchittvā tato devī līlayaiva śarotkarān 
jaghāna turagān bāṇairyantāraṃ caiva vājinām  MarkP 
ciccheda ca dhanuḥ sadyo dhvajaṃ cātisamucchritam 
vivyādha caiva gātreṣu cchinnadhanvānamāśugaiḥ  MarkP 
sa cchinnadhanvā viratho hatāśvo hatasārathiḥ 
abhyadhāvata tāṃ devīṃ khaḍgacarmadharo 'suraḥ  MarkP 
siṃhamāhatya khaḍgena tīkṣṇadhāreṇa mūrdhani 
ājaghāna bhuje savye devīmapyativegavān  MarkP 
tasyāḥ khaḍgo bhujaṃ prāpya paphāla nṛpanandana 
tato jagrāha śūlaṃ sa kopādaruṇalocanaḥ  MarkP 
cikṣepa ca tatastattu bhadrakālyāṃ mahāsuraḥ 
jājvalyamānaṃ tejobhī ravibimbamivāmbarāt  MarkP 
dṛṣṭvā tadāpatacchūlaṃ devī śūlamamuñcata 
tacchūlaṃ śatadhā tena nītaṃ sa ca mahāsuraḥ  MarkP 
hate tasmin mahāvīrye mahiṣasya camūpatau 
ājagāma gajārūḍhaścāmarastridaśārdanaḥ  MarkP 
so 'pi śaktiṃ mumocātha devyāstāmambikā drutam 
huṅkārābhihatāṃ bhūmau pātayāmāsa niṣprabhām  MarkP 
bhagnāṃ śaktiṃ nipatitāṃ dṛṣṭvā krodhasamanvitaḥ 
cikṣepa cāmaraḥ śūlaṃ bāṇaistadapi sācchinat  MarkP 
tataḥ siṃhaḥ samutpatya gajakumbhāntare sthitaḥ 
bāhuyuddhena yuyudhe tenoccaistridaśāriṇā  MarkP 
yudhāyamāno tatastau tu tasmānnāgānmahīṃ gatau 
yuyudhāte 'tisaṃrabdhau prahārairatidāruṇaiḥ  MarkP 
tato vegātkhamutpatya nipatya ca mṛgāriṇā 
karaprahāreṇa śiraścāmarasya pṛthakkṛtam  MarkP 
udagraśca raṇe devyā śilāvṛkṣādibhirhataḥ 
dantamuṣṭitalaiścaiva karālaśca nipātitaḥ  MarkP 
devī kruddhā gadāpātaiścūrṇayāmāsa coddhatam 
vāṣkalaṃ bhindipālena bāṇaistāmraṃ tathāndhakam  MarkP 
ugrāsyamugravīryañca tathaiva ca mahāhanum 
trinetrā ca triśūlena jaghāna parameśvarī  MarkP 
biḍālasyāsinā kāyāt pātayāmāsa vai śiraḥ 
durdharaṃ durmukhaṃ cobhau śarairninye yamakṣayam 
kālaṃ ca kāladaṇḍena kālarātrirapātayat  MarkP 
agradarśanamatyugraiḥ khaḍgapātairatāḍayat 
asinaivāsilomānamacchidat sā raṇotsave 
gaṇaiḥ siṃhena devyā ca jayakṣveḍākṛtotsavaiḥ  MarkP 
evaṃ saṃkṣīyamāṇe tu svasainye mahiṣāsuraḥ 
māhiṣeṇa svarūpeṇa trāsayāmāsa tān gaṇān  MarkP 
kāṃścittuṇḍaprihāreṇa khurakṣepaistathāparān 
lāṅgūlatāḍitāṃścānyān śṛṅgābhyāñca vidāritān  MarkP 
vegena kāṃścidaparān nādena bhramaṇena ca 
niśvāsapavanenānyān pātayāmāsa bhūtale  MarkP 
nipātya pramathānīkamabhyadhāvata so 'suraḥ 
siṃhaṃ hantuṃ mahādevyāḥ kopaṃ cakre tato 'mbikā  MarkP 
so 'pi kopānmahāvīryaḥ khurakṣuṇṇamahītalaḥ 
śṛṅgābhyāṃ parvatānuccaiścikṣepa ca nanāda ca  MarkP 
vegabhramaṇavikṣuṇṇā mahī tasya vyaśīryata 
lāṅgūlenāhataścābdhiḥ plāvayāmāsa sarvataḥ  MarkP 
dhutaśṛṅgavibhinnāśca khaṇḍaṃ khaṇḍaṃ yayurghanā 
śvāsānilāstāḥ śataśo nipeturnabhaso 'calāḥ  MarkP 
iti krodhasamādhmātamāpatāntaṃ mahāsuram 
dṛṣṭvā sā caṇḍikā kopaṃ tadvadhāya tadākarot  MarkP 
sā kṣiptvā tasya vai pāśaṃ taṃ babandha mahāsuram 
tatyāja māhiṣaṃ rūpaṃ so 'pi baddho mahāmṛdhe  MarkP 
tataḥ siṃho 'bhavat sadyo yāvattasyāmbikā śiraḥ 
chinatti tāvatpuruṣaḥ khaḍgapāṇiradṛśyata  MarkP 
tata evāśu puruṣaṃ devī ciccheda sāyakaiḥ 
taṃ khaḍgacarmaṇā sārdhaṃ tataḥ so 'bhūnmahāgajaḥ  MarkP 
kareṇa ca mahāsiṃhaṃ taṃ cakarṣa jagarja ca 
karṣatastu karaṃ devī khaḍgena nirakṛntata  MarkP 
tato mahāsuro bhūyo māhiṣaṃ vapurāsthitaḥ 
tathaiva kṣobhayāmāsa trailokyaṃ sacarācaram  MarkP 
tataḥ kruddhā jaganmātā caṇḍikā pānamuttamam 
papau punaḥ punaścaiva jahāsāruṇalocanā  MarkP 
nanarda cāsuraḥ so 'pi balavīryamadoddhataḥ 
viṣāṇābyāñca cikṣepa caṇḍikāṃ prati bhūdharān  MarkP 
sā ca tān prahitāṃstena cūrṇayantī śarotkaraiḥ 
uvāca taṃ madoddhūtamukharāgākulākṣaram  MarkP 
devyuvāca
garja garja kṣaṇaṃ mūḍha madhu yāvatpibāmyaham 
mayā tvayi hate 'traiva garjiṣyantyāśu devatāḥ  MarkP 
ṛṣiruvāca
evamuktvā samutpatya sārūḍhā taṃ mahāsuram 
pādenākramya kaṇṭhe ca śūlenainamatāḍayat  MarkP 
tataḥ so 'pi padākrāntastayā nijamukhāttataḥ 
ardhaniṣkrānta evāsīd devyā vīryeṇa saṃvṛtaḥ  MarkP 
ardhaniṣkrānta evāsau yudhyamāno mahāsuraḥ 
tayā mahāsinā devyā śiraśchittvā nipātitaḥ  MarkP 
evaṃ sa mahiṣo nāma sasainyaḥ sasuhṛdgaṇaḥ 
trailokyaṃ mohayitvā tu tayā devyā vināśitaḥ  MarkP 
trailokyasthaistadā bhūtairmahiṣe vinipātite 
jayetyuktaṃ tataḥ sarvaiḥ sadevāsuramānavaiḥ  MarkP 
tato hāhākṛtaṃ sarvaṃ daityasainyaṃ nanāśa tat 
praharṣañca paraṃ jagmuḥ sakalā devatāgaṇāḥ  MarkP 
tuṣṭuvustāṃ surā devīṃ saha divyairmaharṣibhiḥ 
jagurgandharvapatayo nanṛtuścāpsarogaṇāḥ  MarkP 
iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe sāvarṇike manvantare devīmāhātmye mahiṣāsuravadho nāma tryaśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
caturaśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ 
ṛṣiruvāca
tataḥ suragaṇāḥ sarve devyā handrapurogamāḥ 
stutimārebhire kartuṃ nihate mahiṣāsure  MarkP 
śakrādayaḥ suragaṇā nihate 'tivīrye
tasmin durātmani surāribale ca devyā 
tāṃ tuṣṭubuḥ praṇatinamraśirodharāṃsā
vāgbhiḥ praharṣapulakodgamacārudehāḥ  MarkP 
devā ūcuḥ
devyā yayā tatamidaṃ jagadātmaśaktyā
niḥ śeṣadevagaṇaśaktisamūhamūrtyā 
tāmambikāmakhiladevamarṣipūjyāṃ
bhaktyā natāḥ sma vidadhātu śubhāni sā naḥ  MarkP 
yasyāḥ prabhāvamatulaṃ bhagavānananto
brahmā haraśca nahi vaktumalaṃ balaṃ ca 
sā caṇḍikākhilajagatparipālanāya
nāśāya cāśubhayasya matiṃ karotu  MarkP 
yā śrīḥ svayaṃ sukṛtināṃ bhavaneṣvalakṣmīḥ
pāpātmanāṃ kṛtadhiyāṃ hṛdayeṣu buddhiḥ 
śraddhāṃ satāṃ kulajanaprabhavasya lajjā
tāṃ tvāṃ natāḥ sma paripālaya devi viśvam  MarkP 
kiṃ varṇayāma tava rūpamacintyametat
kiṃ cātivīryamasurakṣayakāri bhūri 
kiṃ cāhaveṣu caritāni tavādbhutāni
sarveṣu devyasuradevagaṇādikeṣu  MarkP 
hetuḥ samastajagatāṃ triguṇāpi doṣair
na jñāyase hariharādibhirapyapārā 
sarvāśrayākhilamidaṃ jagadaṃśabhūtam
avyākṛtā hi paramā prakṛtistvamādyā  MarkP 
yasyāḥ samastasuratā samudīraṇena
tṛptiṃ priyāti sakaleṣu makheṣu devi 
svāhāsi vai pitṛgaṇasya ca tṛptihetur
uccāryase tvamata eva janaiḥ svadhā ca  MarkP 
yā muktiheturavicintyamahāvratā tvam
abhyasyase suniyatendriyatattvasāraiḥ 
mokṣārthibhirmunibhirastasamastadoṣair
vidyāsi sā bhagavatī paramā hi devi  MarkP 
śabdātmikā suvimalargyajuṣāṃ nidhānam
udgītharamyapadapāṭhavatāṃ ca sāmnām 
devī trayī bhagavatī bhavabhāvanāya
vārtā ca sarvajagatāṃ paramārtihantrī  MarkP 
medhāsi devi viditākhilaśāstrasārā
durgāsi durgabhavasāgaranaurasaṅgā 
śrīḥ kaiṭabhārihṛdayaikakṛtādhivāsā
gaurī tvameva śaśimaulikṛtapratiṣṭhā  MarkP 
īṣatsahāsamamalaṃ paripūrṇacandra
bimbānukāri kanakottamakāntikāntam 
atyadbhutaṃ prahṛtamāttaruṣā tathāpi
vaktraṃ vilokya sahasā mahiṣāsureṇa  MarkP 
dṛṣṭvā tu devi kupitaṃ bhrukuṭīkarālam
udyacchaśāṅkasadṛśacchavi yanna sadyaḥ 
prāṇānmumoca mahīṣastadatīva citraṃ
kairjovyate hi kupitāntakadarśanena  MarkP 
devi prasīda paramā bhavatī bhavāya
sadyo vināśayasi kopavatī kulāni 
vijñātametadadhunaiva yadastametan
nītaṃ balaṃ suvipulaṃ mahiṣāsurasya  MarkP 
te saṃmatā janapadeṣu dhanāni teṣāṃ
teṣāṃ yaśāṃsi na ca sīdati dharmavargaḥ 
dhanyāsta eva nibhṛtātmajabhṛtyadārā
yeṣāṃ sadābhyudayadā bhavatī prasannā  MarkP 
dharmyāṇi devi sakalāni sadaiva karmāṇy
atyādṛtaḥ pratidinaṃ sukṛtī karoti 
svargaṃ prayāti ca tato bhavatīprasādāl
lokatraye 'pi phaladā nanu devi tena  MarkP 
durge smṛtā harasi bhītimaśeṣajantoḥ

dūta uvāca

ṛṣiruvāca
tenājñaptastataḥ śīghraṃ sa daityo dhūmralocanaḥ

sa dṛṣṭvā tāṃ tato devīṃ tuhinācalasaṃsthitām 
jagādoccaiḥ prayāhīti mūlaṃ śumbhaniśumbhayoḥ  MarkP

daityeśvareṇa prahito balavān balasaṃvṛtaḥ 
balānnayasi māmevaṃ tataḥ kiṃ te karomyaham  MarkP 
ṛṣiruvāca
ityuktaḥ so 'bhyadhāvattāmasuro dhūmralocanaḥ 
huṅkāreṇaiva taṃ bhasma sā cakārāmbikā tataḥ  MarkP 
atha kruddhaṃ mahāsainyamasurāṇāṃ tathāmbikā 
vavarṣa sāyakaistīkṣṇaistathā śaktiparaśvadhaiḥ  MarkP 
tato dhutasaṭaḥ kopāt kṛtvā nādaṃ subhairavam 
papātāsurasenāyāṃ siṃho devyāḥ svavāhanaḥ  MarkP 
kāṃścit karaprahāreṇa daityānāsyena cāparān 
ākramya cādhareṇānyān sa jaghāna mahāsurān  MarkP 
keṣāñcit pāṭayāmāsa nakhaiḥ koṣṭhāni kesarī 
tathā talaprihāreṇa śirāṃsi kṛtavān pṛthak  MarkP 
vicchinnabāhuśirasaḥ sṛtāstena tathāpare 
papau ca rudhiraṃ koṣṭhādanyeṣāṃ dhutakesaraḥ  MarkP 
kṣaṇena tadbalaṃ sarvaṃ kṣayaṃ nītaṃ mahātmanā 
tena kesariṇā devyā vāhanenātikopinā  MarkP 
śrutvā tamasuraṃ devyā nihataṃ dhūmralocanam 
balaṃ ca kṣayitaṃ kṛtstraṃ devīkesariṇā tataḥ  MarkP 
cukopa daityādhipatiḥ śumbhaḥ prasphuritādharaḥ 
ājñāpayāmāsa ca tau caṇḍamuṇḍau mahāsurau  MarkP 
he caṇḍa he muṇḍa balairbahubhiḥ parivāritau 
tatra gacchata gatvā ca sā samānīyatāṃ laghu  MarkP 
keśeṣvākṛṣya baddhvā vā yadi vaḥ saṃśayo yudhi 
tadāśeṣāyudhaiḥ sarvairasurairvinihanyatām  MarkP 
tasyāṃ hatāyāṃ duṣṭāyāṃ siṃhe ca vinipātite 
śīghramāgamyatāṃ baddhvā gṛhītvā tāmathāmbikām  MarkP 
iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyamahāpurāṇe sāvarṇike manvantare devīmāhātmye dhūmralocanavadho nāma ṣaḍaśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
saptaśītitamādhyāyaḥ

ājñaptāste tato daityāścaṇḍamuṇḍapurogamāḥ 
caturaṅgabalopetā yayurabhyudyatāyudhāḥ  MarkP 
dadṛśuste tato devīmīṣaddhāsāṃ vyavasthitām 
siṃhasyopari śailendraśṛṅge mahati kāñcane  MarkP

ākṛṣṭacāpāsidharāstathānye satsamīpagāḥ  MarkP 
tataḥ kopaṃ cakāroccairambikā tānarīn prati

bhrukuṭīkuṭilāttasyā lalāṭaphalakād drutam

tatrāpi sā nirādhārā yuyudhe tena caṇḍikā  MarkP

utpātya bhrāmayāmāsa cikṣepa dharaṇītale  MarkP 
sa kṣipto dharaṇīṃ prāpya muṣṭimudyamya vegitaḥ 
abhyadhāvata duṣṭātmā caṇḍikānidhanecchayā  MarkP 
tamāyāntaṃ tato devī sarvadaityajaneśvaram

babhūvurnihate tasmin gandharvā lalitaṃ jaguḥ  MarkP

ṛṣiruvāca
devyā hate tatra mahāsurendre

devā ūcuḥ

tato 'hamakhilaṃ lokamātmadehasamudbhavaiḥ

devyuvāca
ebhiḥ stavaiśca māṃ nityaṃ stoṣyate yaḥ samāhitaḥ 
tasyāhaṃ sakalāṃ bādhāṃ nāśayiṣyāmyasaṃśayam  MarkP 
madhukaiṭabhānāśaṃ ca mahiṣāsuraghātanam 
kīrtayiṣyinti ye tadvad vadhaṃ śumbhaniśumbhayoḥ  MarkP 
aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ navamyāṃ caikacetasaḥ 
stoṣyanti caiva ye bhaktyā mama māhātmyamuttamam  MarkP 
na teṣāṃ duṣkṛtaṃ kiñcid duṣkṛtotthā na cāpadaḥ 
bhaviṣyati na dāridrayaṃ na caiveṣṭaviyojanam  MarkP 
śatruto na bhayaṃ tasya dasyuto vā na rājataḥ 
na śastrānalatoyaughāt kadācit sambhaviṣyati  MarkP 
tasmānmamaitanmāhātmyaṃ paṭhitavyaṃ sahāhitaiḥ 
śrotavyaṃ ca sadā bhaktyā paraṃ svastyayanaṃ mahat  MarkP 
upasargānaśeṣāṃstu mahāmārīsamudbhavān 
tathā trividhamutpātaṃ māhātmyaṃ śamayenmama  MarkP 
yatraitat paṭhyate samyaṅnityamāyatane mama 
sadā na tadvimokṣyāmi sāṃnidhyaṃ tatra me sthitam  MarkP 
balipradāne pūjāyāmagnikārye mahotsave 
sarvaṃ mamaitaccaritamuccāryaṃ śrāvyameva ca  MarkP 
jānatājānatā vāpi balipūjāṃ tathā kṛtām 
pratīcchiṣyāmyahaṃ prītyā vahnihomaṃ tathā kṛtam  MarkP 
śaratkāle mahāpūjā kriyate yā ca vārṣikī 
tasyāṃ mamaitanmāhātmyaṃ śrutvā bhaktisamanvitaḥ  MarkP 
sarvabādhāvinirmṛkto dhanadhānyasamanvitaḥ 
manuṣyo matprasādena bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ  MarkP 
śrutvā mamaitanmāhātmyaṃ tathotpattīḥ pṛthak śubhāḥ 
parākramaṃ ca yuddheṣu jāyate nirbhayaḥ pumān  MarkP 
ripavaḥ saṃkṣayaṃ yānti kalyāṇaṃ copapadyate 
nandate ca kulaṃ puṃsāṃ māhātmyaṃ mama śṛṇvatām  MarkP 
śāntikarmaṇi sarvatra tathā duḥ svapnadarśane 
grahapīḍāsu cogrāsu māhātmyaṃ śṛṇuyānmama  MarkP 
upasargāḥ śamaṃ yānti grahapīḍāśca dāruṇāḥ 
duḥ svapnaṃ ca nṛbhirdṛṣṭaṃ susvapnamupajāyate  MarkP 
bālagrahābhibhūtānāṃ bālānāṃ śāntikārakam 
saṃghātabhede ca nṛṇāṃ maitrīkaraṇamuttamam  MarkP 
durvṛttānāmaśeṣāṇāṃ balahānikaraṃ param 
rakṣobhūtapiśācānāṃ paṭhanādeva nāśanam  MarkP 
sarvaṃ mamaitanmāhātmyaṃ mama sannidhikārakam  MarkP 
paśupuṣpārghyadhūpaiśca gandhadīpaistathottamaiḥ 
viprāṇāṃ bhojanairhemaiḥ prokṣaṇīyairaharniśam  MarkP

śrutaṃ harati pāpāni tathā'rogyaṃ prayacchati 
rakṣāṃ karoti bhūtebhyo janmanāṃ kīrtanaṃ mama  MarkP 
yuddheṣu caritaṃ yanme duṣṭadaityanibarhaṇam 
tasmin śrute vairikṛtaṃ bhayaṃ puṃsāṃ na jāyate  MarkP 
yuṣmābhiḥ stutayo yāśca yāśca brahmarṣibhiḥ kṛtāḥ 
brahmaṇā ca kṛtāstāstu prayacchanti śubhāṃ gatim  MarkP 
araṇye prāntare vāpi dāvāgniparivāritaḥ
